(trg)="201"> XHTML Documents which follow the guidelines set forth in Appendix C , " HTML Compatibility Guidelines " may be labeled with the Internet Media Type " text / html " [ RFC2854 ] , as they are compatible with most HTML browsers .
(trg)="202"> Those documents , and any other document conforming to this specification , may also be labeled with the Internet Media Type " application / xhtml + xml " as defined in [ RFC3236 ] . ↑ " RFC 2119 : Key words for use in RFCs to Indicate Requirement Levels " .

(src)="80716"> HyperText Markup Language , commonly referred to as HTML , is the standard markup language used to create web pages .
(src)="80717"> Along with CSS , and JavaScript , HTML is a cornerstone technology , used by most websites to create visually engaging web pages , user interfaces for web applications , and user interfaces for many mobile applications.[1 ] Web browsers can read HTML files and render them into visible or audible web pages .
(src)="80718"> HTML describes the structure of a website semantically along with cues for presentation , making it a markup language , rather than a programming language .

(src)="80722"> Johann van Beethoven[1][2 ] ( c.
(src)="80723"> 1739 or 1740[3][4 ] – 18 December 1792 ) was a German musician , teacher , and singer who sang in the chapel of the Archbishop of Cologne , whose court was at Bonn .
(src)="80724"> He is best known as the father of the celebrated composer Ludwig van Beethoven ( 1770–1827 ) .

(src)="80775"> Ronaldo began his club career playing for Sporting CP , before signing with Manchester United at age 18 in 2003 .
(src)="80776"> After winning his first trophy , the FA Cup , during his first season in England , he helped United win three successive Premier League titles , a UEFA Champions League title , and a FIFA Club World Cup .
(src)="80777"> By age 23 , he had received Ballon d'Or and FIFA World Player of the Year nominations .
(src)="80778"> He was the subject of the most expensive association football transfer when he moved from Manchester United to Real Madrid in 2009 in a transfer worth €94  million ( $132  million ) .
(src)="80779"> In Spain , he has since won one La Liga title , two Copas del Rey , two Champions League titles , and two Club World Cups .
(src)="80780"> Ronaldo holds the record for most goals scored in a single UEFA Champions League season , having scored 17 goals in the 2013–14 season .

(src)="80782"> He is the only player in the history of football to score more than 50 goals in a season on six consecutive occasions .
(src)="80783"> In 2015 , Ronaldo became the all-time top goalscorer in the UEFA Champions League , and he also became Real Madrid 's all-time leading goalscorer .
(src)="80784"> He is the second highest goalscorer in La Liga history behind Lionel Messi , his perceived career rival .

(src)="80785"> Ronaldo made his international debut for Portugal in August 2003 , at the age of 18 .
(src)="80786"> He is Portugal 's most capped player of all time with over 130 caps , and has participated in seven major tournaments : four UEFA European Championships ( 2004 , 2008 , 2012 and 2016 ) and three FIFA World Cups ( 2006 , 2010 and 2014 ) .
(src)="80787"> He is the first Portuguese player to reach 50 international goals , making him Portugal 's all-time top goalscorer .
(src)="80788"> He scored his first international goal in Euro 2004 and helped Portugal reach the final .

(src)="80790"> In November 2014 , Ronaldo became the all-time top scorer in the UEFA European Championship ( including qualifying ) with 23 goals .
(src)="80791"> At Euro 2016 , he became the most capped player of all-time in the tournament , the first player to score at four consecutive European Championship finals , and also equalled Michel Platini 's all-time record for most goals scored in the competition .
(src)="80792"> Ronaldo lifted the trophy after Portugal defeated France in the final , and he received the Silver Boot as the second-highest goalscorer of the tournament .

(trg)="307"> At Euro 2016 , he became the most capped player of all-time in the tournament , the first player to score at four consecutive European Championship finals , and also equalled Michel Platini ' s all-time record for most goals scored in the competition .
(trg)="308"> Ronaldo lifted the trophy after Portugal defeated France in the final , and he received the Silver Boot as the second-highest goalscorer of the tournament .
(src)="80793"> Roger Federer ( born 8 August 1981 ) is a Swiss professional tennis player who is currently ranked world No. 5 by the Association of Tennis Professionals (ATP).[4 ] Federer turned professional in 1998 and was continuously ranked in the top 10 from October 2002 to November 2016.[5 ] Federer has won 18 Grand Slam singles titles , the most in history for a male tennis player , and held the world No. 1 spot in the ATP rankings for a record total of 302 weeks .
(trg)="309"> Roger Federer ( born 8 August 1981 ) is a Swiss professional tennis player who is currently ranked world No. 5 by the Association of Tennis Professionals ( ATP ) . [ 4 ] Federer turned professional in 1998 and was continuously ranked in the top 10 from October 2002 to November 2016 . [ 5 ] Federer has won 18 Grand Slam singles titles , the most in history for a male tennis player , and held the world No. 1 spot in the ATP rankings for a record total of 302 weeks .

(trg)="1126"> Notes
(src)="81611"> Malcolm Bligh Turnbull ( born 24 October 1954 ) is the 29th and current Prime Minister of Australia .
(src)="81612"> He first served as parliamentary leader of the Liberal Party of Australia and as opposition leader from 2008 to 2009 , and became parliamentary leader and Prime Minister after defeating Tony Abbott at the 2015 Liberal leadership spill .
(src)="81613"> The Turnbull Government was re-elected at the 2016 federal election though with a bare one-seat majority .
(trg)="1127"> Malcolm Bligh Turnbull ( janam : 24 October 1954 ) , Australia ke 29th aur abhi ke Prime Minister hai .

(trg)="1129"> 2015 me uu Tony Abbott  ke harae ke Prime Minister banaa .
(trg)="1130"> Turnbull ke sarkar 2016 ke election ek seat ke majority se jiitis .

(trg)="1364"> The form of chess most people know — which is sometimes referred to as Western chess , orthodox chess , or orthochess — is itself just one of many that have been played throughout history . 
(src)="81852"> Chess is a two-player strategy board game played on a chessboard , a checkered gameboard with 64  squares arranged in an 8×8 grid.[1 ] The game is played by millions of people worldwide and is believed to be originated from India.[2 ]
(trg)="1365"> Chess is a two-player strategy board game played on a chessboard , a checkered gameboard with 64  squares arranged in an 8 × 8 grid . [ 1 ] The game is played by millions of people worldwide and is believed to be originated from India . [ 2 ]
(src)="81853"> References

(src)="81854"> Notes
(trg)="1367"> Notes
(src)="81855"> The Bay of Plenty or Te Moana-a-Toi ( Māori ) is a large bight in the northern coast of New Zealand 's North Island .
(src)="81856"> It stretches from the Coromandel Peninsula in the west to Cape Runaway in the east , a wide stretch of some 259  km of open coastline .
(src)="81857"> The Bay of Plenty Region is situated around this body of water , also incorporating several large islands in the bay .
(src)="81858"> The bay was named by James Cook after he noticed the abundant food supplies at several Māori villages there , in stark contrast to the earlier observations he had made in Poverty Bay .
(trg)="1368"> Bay of Plenty nai to  Te Moana-a-Toi ( Māori ) , New Zealand ke North Island me ek barraa Bay hai .
(trg)="1369"> Ii West me Coromandel Peninsula  se East me Cape Runaway talak 259  km ke coastline hai .
(trg)="1370"> Ii bay ke James Cook  naam diis rahaa , kaaheki uu hian ke Maori gaon me dher khaana dekhis .
(src)="81859"> Peter Craig Dutton ( born 18 November 1970),[1 ] Australian politician , has been a Liberal member of the Australian House of Representatives representing the Division of Dickson , Queensland since the November 2001 federal election when he defeated high-profile sitting Labor member Cheryl Kernot .
(src)="81860"> Dutton was the Minister for Health and the Minister for Sport from 18 September 2013 and Minister for Immigration and Border Protection from 21 December 2014 in the Abbott Government .
(src)="81861"> Dutton retained his portfolio in the Turnbull Government.[2 ] On 18 July 2017 , he was named Minister for Home Affairs , a newly created portfolio giving him oversight of ASIO , the AFP and Border Force.[3 ] He previously served as the Minister for Workforce Participation and Minister for Revenue and Assistant Treasurer in the Howard Government .
(src)="81862"> Dutton has been touted as a future Liberal leader.[4][5][6][7 ]
(trg)="1371"> Peter Craig Dutton ( janam : 18 November 1970 ) , [ 1 ] ek Australian politician hai , jon ki Australia ke House of Representatives ke Liberal member hai .
(trg)="1372"> 2001 ke election me uu Dickson Constituency se pahila dafe chuna gais rahaa .
(trg)="1373"> Dutton , 18 September 2013 se Minister of Health rahaa .
(trg)="1374"> December 2014 se uu Minister for Immigration and Border Protection  rahaa .. [ 2 ] 18 July 2017 ke uske Minister for Home Affairs , jisme ASIO , the AFP aur Border Force rahii [ 3 ] , hai. pahile ke sarkar me uu  Minister for Workforce Participation and Minister for Revenue and Assistant Treasurer  rahaa .
(trg)="1375"> Dutton ke aage ke Liberal leader maana jaawe hai . [ 4 ] [ 5 ] [ 6 ] [ 7 ]

(src)="82544"> Pregnancy , also known as gestation , is the time during which one or more offspring develops inside a woman.[4 ] A multiple pregnancy involves more than one offspring , such as with twins.[12 ] Pregnancy can occur by sexual intercourse or assisted reproductive technology.[6 ] Childbirth typically occurs around 40  weeks from the last menstrual period (LMP).[4][5 ] This is just over nine  lunar months , where each month is about 29½ days.[4][5 ] When measured from conception it is about 38 weeks .
(src)="82545"> An embryo is the developing offspring during the first eight weeks following conception , after which , the term fetus is used until birth.[5 ] Symptoms of early pregnancy may include missed periods , tender breasts , nausea and vomiting , hunger , and frequent urination.[1 ] Pregnancy may be confirmed with a pregnancy test.[7 ]
(trg)="2053"> Pregnancy , also known as gestation , is the time during which one or more offspring develops inside a woman . [ 4 ] A multiple pregnancy involves more than one offspring , such as with twins . [ 12 ] Pregnancy can occur by sexual intercourse or assisted reproductive technology . [ 6 ] Childbirth typically occurs around 40  weeks from the last menstrual period ( LMP ) . [ 4 ] [ 5 ] This is just over nine  lunar months , where each month is about 29 ½ days . [ 4 ] [ 5 ] When measured from conception it is about 38 weeks .
(trg)="2054"> An embryo is the developing offspring during the first eight weeks following conception , after which , the term fetus is used until birth . [ 5 ] Symptoms of early pregnancy may include missed periods , tender breasts , nausea and vomiting , hunger , and frequent urination . [ 1 ] Pregnancy may be confirmed with a pregnancy test . [ 7 ]

(trg)="2055"> References
(src)="82547"> Ram Nath Kovind ( born 1 October 1945 ) is an Indian politician who is the 14th and current President of India .
(src)="82548"> He served as the  35th Governor of Bihar  from 2015 to 2017[2 ] and was a Member of Parliament ,  Rajya Sabha  from 1994 to 2006 .
(src)="82549"> He was a leader of the Bharatiya Janata Party ( BJP ) .
(src)="82550"> Kovind was nominated as a presidential candidate by the ruling NDA coalition and won the 2017 presidential election , becoming the second Dalit to be elected to the post of president.[3 ] He assumed office on 25 July 2017 .
(trg)="2056"> Ram Nath Kovind ( janam : 1 October 1945 ) India  ke ek politician hai jon ki 14th aur abhi ke President hai .
(trg)="2057"> Uu 2015 se 2017 talak Bjiar ke  35th Governor  rahaa [ 2 ]  aur 1994 se 2006 talak Rajya Sabha  ke member rahaa .
(trg)="2058"> Uu  Bharatiya Janata Party ( BJP ) ke ek neta hai .
(trg)="2059"> Kovind ke ruling NDA coalition 2017 presidential election  ke khatir nominate karis rahaa , aur uu duusra  Dalit  hai jon ki President banaa . [ 3 ]  Uu  25 July 2017 se President ke kaam suruu karis .

(trg)="2120"> Dr. Mahendra Reddy  Fiji ke ek politician aur House of Representatives ke member hai .
(trg)="2121"> Uu Fiji ke iMinister for Education , National Heritage , Culture and Arts rahaa . [ 1 ]
(src)="82615"> Reddy was an award-winning scholarship student at the University of the South Pacific and the University of Hawaii .
(src)="82616"> He did his Master of Science Degree and PhD in Agriculture and Resource Economics on a Fulbright Scholarship on an East-West Centre Fellowship at the University of Hawaii .
(src)="82617"> He taught Economics at the University of the South Pacific , becoming a Lecturer in Development Studies in 1998 and getting promoted to Senior lecturer in 2005 .
(src)="82618"> In 2007 , he became the Associate Dean of the Faculty of Business and Economics and Associate Professor of Economics .
(src)="82619"> In 2008 , he became the Head of the USP School of Economics before being transferred to the Fiji Institute of Technology in October as the Dean of the Faculty of Commerce , Hospitality and Tourism Studies.[2 ]
(trg)="2122"> Reddy ,  University of the South Pacific  aur the University of Hawaii  ke ek award winning student rahaa .

(trg)="2140"> References
(src)="82638"> Sarojini Naidu ( 1879–1949 ) , also known by the sobriquet Nightingale of India,[1 ] was a poet and politician.Sarojini Naidu served as the first governor of the United Provinces of Agra and Oudh from 1947 to 1949 .
(src)="82639"> She was the first woman to become the governor of an Indian state.[2 ] She was the second to become the president of the Indian National Congress in 1925 and the first woman in India to do so.[3 ]
(trg)="2141"> Sarojini Naidu ( 1879 – 1949 ) , jiske India ke Nghtingale , ke naam se bhi jaana jaawat rahaa , United Provinces ke pahila Governor rahii .
(trg)="2142"> Uu pahila aurat rahii jon ki ek India ke state ke Governor bais rahaa .
(trg)="2143"> Uu Indian National Congress ke duusra President rahis .

(trg)="2201"> Sara Loren Born : December 11 , 1985 ( 1985-12-11 ) ( age  32 ) Kuwait City , Kuwait Occupation : Actress
(src)="82700"> Sara Loren ( Urdu : ساره لورين‬‎ ; born as Mona Lizza Hussain ) , is a Pakistani actress and model.[1 ]
(trg)="2202"> Sara Loren ( Urdu : ساره لورين ‬ ‎ ; janma naam  Mona Lizza Hussain ) , iek  Pakistani actress and model hai . [ 1 ]
(src)="82701"> Loren made her film debut in the 2010 Pooja Bhatt 's romantic thriller film Kajraare opposite Himesh Reshammiya and later played seductress Nisha in the 2013 film Murder 3 .
(src)="82702"> The following year she starred in Yasir Nawaz 's Anjuman for which she won the Tarang Housefull Awards—Best Actress in a Leading Role.[2 ]
(trg)="2203"> Loren ka debut hua 2013 mai [ [ Pooja Bhatt ] ] ka film ke zariye .

(src)="82712"> Murder 3 is an Indian psychological thriller film and the sequel to the 2011 film , Murder 2 .
(src)="82713"> Directed by Vishesh Bhatt and produced by Mukesh Bhatt from Vishesh Films .
(src)="82714"> This is the third installment in the series and unlike its predecessors , this edition is an official remake - of the Colombian thriller The Hidden Face .
(src)="82715"> Murder 3 was released on 15 February 2013 to mixed reviews .
(src)="82716"> The film performed moderately well at the box office.[1 ]
